The weakest part of the plot is... the core of the plot -  those monsters who have keen ears.   If the creature can hear a tiny sound kilometers away, that means the loud sound will definitely hurt it. The very loud sound will simply damage it`s hearing organs and, due to creatures` blindness, make them completely disabled. Did you ever hear the sound of tank engine in a close range? - I did. It is *very loud* . Same for the jets, ships, shots and explosions.  So all that ''battle'' between the aliens and men`s modern armies does not make any sense - aliens will lose before humans make their first shot.
